<p style="font-size: 1.7em; line-height: 1.9em; margin-bottom: 80px;">Map an organizations attack surface with a virtual <i>dumpster dive*</i> of the DNS records associated with the target organization.</p>
<p style="font-size: 1.2em; color: #fff;">*DUMPSTER DIVING: The practice of sifting refuse from an office or technical installation to extract confidential data, especially security-compromising information.<br><span style="font-size: 0.9;"><i>Dictionary.com</i></span></p>

<div class="container" style="text-align: left; margin-top: 80px; margin-bottom: 80px;">

<h2 style="font-size: 1.8em;">Frequently Asked Questions</h2>

<h4 style="margin-top: 30px;">How can I take my security assessments to the next level?</h4>

<p>The company behind DNSDumpster is <a href="https://hackertarget.com/" title="Online Vulnerability Scanners">hackertarget.com</a> where we provide online hosted access to trusted open source security testing tools. Save time and headaches by incorporating hosted scanners into your vulnerability assessment process.</p>

<h4>What data does DNSDumpster use?</h4>

<p>No brute force subdomain enumeration is used as is common in dns recon tools that enumerate subdomains. We use open source intelligence resources to query for related domain data. It is then compiled into an actionable resource for both attackers and defenders of Internet facing systems.</P>
<P>More than a simple <a href="https://hackertarget.com/dns-lookup/" title="Online DNS Lookup">DNS lookup</a> this tool will discover those hard to find sub-domains and web hosts. The search relies on data from our crawls of the Alexa Top 1 Million sites, Search Engines, Common Crawl, Certificate Transparency, Max Mind, Team Cymru, Shodan and <a href="https://scans.io/" style="text-decoration: underline;">scans.io</a>.</P>

<h4>I have hit the host limit, do you have a PRO option?</h4>

<P>Over at <a href="https://hackertarget.com/">hackertarget.com</a> there's a tool we call <a href="https://hackertarget.com/domain-profiler/">domain profiler</a>. This compiles data similiar to DNSDumpster with up to 40K results. With a STARTER membership you have access to the domain profiler tool for 12 months. Once the years membership expires you will revert to BASIC member status, however access to Domain Profiler and Basic Nmap scans continue. The BASIC access does not expire.</P>

<h4>What are some other resources and tools for learning more?</h4>

<P>There are some great open source recon frameworks that have been developed over the past couple of years. In addition tools such as <b>Metasploit</b> and <b>Nmap</b> include various modules for enumerating DNS. Check our <a href="https://dnsdumpster.com/footprinting-reconnaissance/">Getting Started with Footprinting</a> for more information.</P>

</div>

<script>
var gdpData = {

"EU" : 11,

"AP" : 12,

"CN" : 5,

"US" : 131,

};
    $(function(){
$('#world-map').vectorMap({
  map: 'world_mill_en',
  backgroundColor: '#333333',
  zoomButtons : false,
  series: {
    regions: [{
      values: gdpData,
      scale: ['#00CC00', '#008400'],
      normalizeFunction: 'polynomial'
    }]
  },
  onRegionTipShow: function(e, el, code){
    if (typeof gdpData[code] !=="undefined"){
    el.html(el.html()+' <br>Hosts Found : '+gdpData[code]);
    } 
  }
});
    });
  </script>
